* Can the Minister confirm that, for the purpose of increasing the impact of their terror campaign, the Cambodian communists forbid exit from Cambodia and, as a matter of routine, execute any Cambodian <span class="highlight">refugees</span> whom they can apprehend? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761208_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-11-0)

* Has the Government any details of the recent incident when 26 Cambodian <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, including children, were returned across the border by the Thai authorities and are said to have been forthwith beheaded by the Khmer Rouge, that is, the Cambodian communists? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761208_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-11-0)

* I rise this evening to discuss the plight of Chilean <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who face deportation at the hands of this Government. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761208_reps_30_hor102/#debate-41)

* He has been asked several questions during recent months about the entitlement of Lebanese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> to come to Australia and the facilities for interviewing them overseas. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-11-0)

* Further, I raise the issue of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> or quasi-<span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#debate-44)

* The Government's policy towards the entry of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> is governed by its obligations as a party to the United Nations Convention on the Status of <span class="highlight">Refugees</span> and its acknowledgement that as a member of the international community it must accept a share of responsibility in refugee and quasi-refugee situations which often involve personal danger and loss of human dignity, basic rights and means of livelihood. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-86-1)

* In accord with this approach the Government is prepared to do what it can to facilitate the resettlement of those <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who can be integrated into the Australian community as well as others who though not in a strict sense <span class="highlight">refugees</span> have been displaced and are the victims of severe privation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-86-1)

* The extent to which Australia can participate in these types of projects must allow for special arrangements to be made to interview applicants and must take into account the ability of any particular group of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> or displaced persons to integrate into the community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-86-1)

* Any proposal to admit <span class="highlight">refugees</span> must be dealt with on a global basis and does not permit specific groups to be dealt with in isolation to the exclusion of other groups who may be seen as eligible to benefit from Australia's refugee policy. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-86-1)

* The procedures adopted for the selection and movement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and displaced persons whose entry has been approved in principle ensure that the standard migrant criteria are not imposed as this could effectively deny to the persons concerned the resettlement opportunities which the Government has offered. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-86-1)

* Health and character standards are insisted on but allowance is made for the parlous situation in which the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> find themselves and their inability to comply strictly with rules related to occupational skills, etc. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-86-1)

* The criteria used to determine eligibility for entry to Australia as <span class="highlight">refugees</span> allow for the chances of resettlement in the country in which the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> find themselves, the degree of support which would be forthcoming in that country, alternative opportunities for resettlement elsewhere more readily on the basis of language or closer association and Australia 's ability to integrate the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> at any given dme. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19761209_reps_30_hor102/#subdebate-86-1)

* Deal sympathetically with the hopes and aims of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, especially from countries who have been recent Australian allies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770309_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-4-0)

* Where was their Government when the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from those countries sought entry to Australia? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770309_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-29-2)

* I notice that the Senate committee looking into this matter, which include Labor members, has reported to the other place that there was deliberate delay and deliberate action by the former Labor Government to prevent <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from that part of the world from coming to Australia, because it sought to cover the shame that it had helped to create. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770309_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-29-2)

* -In October 1976 I rose in this House to deplore the plight of Lebanese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> stranded in Nicosia and other points around the Mediterranean. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-24-0)

* The total needed to sustain Lebanese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> runs into millions of dollars. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-24-0)

* It is true that many hundreds of category B <span class="highlight">refugees</span>- brothers and sisters and others who fall into that category of Australian Lebanesecame to Australia in the first heady days of the relaxed entry criteria when this Government was trying to demonstrate that it had the right approach to the refugee problem. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-24-0)

* The price of that bungling is the despair of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and the heavy financial burden on the Lebanese community in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-24-0)

* The Lebanese community here regards this matter as one of extreme urgency, as it would relieve the suffering of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and would lift from their relatives the burden of having to pay the huge cost of supporting them in Cyprus. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-24-0)

* As I have said, the staff have worked diligently and under the most difficult conditions to cope with the situation, which is impossible given the number of distressed <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-24-0)

* Yet from what I can ascertain these committees are very disturbed, on the one hand, at the length of time which <span class="highlight">refugees</span> have had to languish in places such as Nicosia and, on the other hand, at the current extraordinarily large number of rejections on medical grounds. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-24-0)

* These <span class="highlight">refugees</span> should not be allowed to languish on Cyprus or anywhere else because Australia is too niggardly to send more immigration officers or more medical officers to Nicosia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* He insists upon calling them <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* In a very real sense they are, except, if one has to be precise, they do not come within the definition of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> as accepted by the United Nations High Commissioner for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* For purposes of entry to Australia, Australia has treated people disadvantaged by the situation in the Lebanon as quasi-<span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* I mention this because we should look at this entire problem of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> or quasi-<span class="highlight">refugees</span> not in relation only to one point in the world but in relation to the entire refugee or quasi-refugee situation which exists. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* It is rather interesting that the Opposition has understandably placed great emphasis on the Lebanese situation- a situation which the Government has recognised consistently and has done something about- but not once has the spokesman for the Opposition mentioned the plight of Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who, at this stage, are in parlous circumstances in refugee camps in Thailand and Malaysia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* Australia has taken into its care a large number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> or quasi-<span class="highlight">refugees</span>- a number that more than favourably compares with the numbers that have gone to other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* What has happened throughout the world is that the Canadians have in the main taken <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who already had relatives living in Canada. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* It left us with no immigration policy properly referrable to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* The report of the Senate Standing Committee on Foreign Affairs and Defence on the Australian refugee problem which was recently published- the Committee included members of the Austraiian Labor Party- said that the former Government deliberately delayed bringing Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> into Australia in order to minimise the number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> with which Australia would have to concern itself. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* If there has been any selectivity in caring for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> around the world it has been by this Government in its approach towards people whose homes were devastated in the Friuli region of Italy or towards those who were the victims of the tragic events in Cyprus. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* Everybody remembers the shortlived operation at the Netherlands Embassy in Damascus in Syria where facilities were made available for a short time for the processing of applications of Lebanese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* The honourable member for Melbourne has been completely irresponsible in trying to blame the Minister for the flood of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> into Cyprus. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-25-3)

* Reports of mass, indiscriminate killings have now come to Australia from Fretilin, which alleged that the Indonesians were 'massacring' the population and from Chinese sources, including from Taiwan, which claimed that the Chinese minority in East Timor bore the brunt of much of the indiscriminate killing in the territory from Timor Democratic Union- UDT- <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Portugal, many of whom claim actually to have witnessed atrocities of a disturbing kind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770316_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-22-0)

* Attention should be drawn to the situation in respect of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770316_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-22-0)

* Australia has taken many <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from the world's trouble spots. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770316_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-22-0)

* I emphasise this because, although the Government has done a great deal to receive <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, I believe it should do more. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770316_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-22-0)

* Since coming to office this Government has taken many initiatives in regard to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, exerting pressure for the withdrawal of Indonesian troops, and sending a special representative to Timor to mention a few. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770316_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-22-0)

* The Paper also mentions <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* I do not think that in a 1 5 minute speech one has time even to begin to talk about <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* The whole question of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> has to hinge on the moral question apart from all other questions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* I am afraid that I must say again that the attitude of the previous Government to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who fought beside us in South-East Asia did not hinge on any sort of moral issues at all. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* I believe that political <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, particularly those from countries such as East Timor or Chile, should be allowed to come here. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* Australia's obligations, moral and practical, with respect to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* In dealing with the questions of Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, it says: [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* It is good that two Liberal MPs have pressed the Government to accept more Vietnamese and Cambodian <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, but disappointing that  Mr MacKellar  sounds so unsympathetic. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* As at 3 1 January this year there were 77 825 Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* At the moment they are in Thailand as temporary <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* We had a deplorable record under the Whitlam Government where, notwithstanding knowledge of the impending fall of Saigon and notwithstanding the knowledge that <span class="highlight">refugees</span> were going to try to get into this country and that we would need to get them out of Vietnam before Saigon fell, the Whitlam Government's proud refugee intake was 76 people. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* At this very moment, as I said, there are over 77 000 of these <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Thai refugee camps. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* Twenty-six Cambodian <span class="highlight">refugees</span> were blindfolded and put across the border into Cambodia where they were shot immediately. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* We cannot ignore, and I know that we have a Minister who will not ignore, the plight of those Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and Australia's moral responsibility for them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* Like the honourable member for St George  (Mr Neil),  I deplore the deafening silence of those who were so active during the Vietnam war, those who marched through the streets and who are now silent on the question of Australia's obligations to those <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* I also propose a regular intake of these <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and an extension of the system of sponsorship of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> by church organisations and other groups. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* He was just talking about the Labor Government's attitude to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-26-1)

* Caring for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from brutality and murder around the world is a major problem for all free nations. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* This is shown by the announcement during the week by the Government of details of the number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who have come to Australia in recent times. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* These facts effectively counter the unfair criticism from some people whose proper concern for the welfare of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> has led them to the wrong conclusion that Australia is not doing enough. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* The facts show that in the last 2 years the number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> or people of similar status arriving in Australia as a result of crises around the world includes about 6000 Lebanese, 2550 Vietnamese, 2580 Timorese, 6500 Cypriots, 1020 Chileans, 600 Laotians, 400 Cambodians and 600 Russian Jews, White Russians and other groups. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* But for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> the situation is totally different. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* As a result, a major backup service is needed to cater for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> when they arrive here. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* This is an extraordinary statement from a Party which, when in office, had a deplorable record on <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* The present Government has not only significantly increased the refugee intake but also is improving the nation's capacity to cope with the special requirements of these <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* This has been helped by the findings of last December's report by the Senate Standing Committee on Foreign Affairs and Defence on the plight and circumstances of Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770324_reps_30_hor104/#debate-39)

* The Prime Minister noted that another aspect of the human suffering caused by the conflict had been the plight of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> - [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770330_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-30-0)

* The  President  and the Prime Minister agreed that officials of their two countries would be meeting to resolve the problem of their <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770330_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-30-0)

* The surprising aspect is that the communique issued after the visit of the Prime Minister  (Mr Malcolm Fraser)  to Indonesia in 1976 referred to these people as <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770330_reps_30_hor104/#debate-34)

* There may not seem to be a great deal of difference in the words 'evacuees' and '<span class="highlight">refugees</span>', but there is a difference. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770330_reps_30_hor104/#debate-34)

* I know how the Public Service operates and I know the constraints which will be placed on people who are classed as evacuees rather than <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770330_reps_30_hor104/#debate-34)

* I ask the Minister whether he will apply the same conditions to the families of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>- and they are <span class="highlight">refugees</span>- presently in Australia as he applied to the people from wartorn Lebanon. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770330_reps_30_hor104/#debate-34)

* We have only to witness the wicked campaign whipped up by Government supporters on aid given via the United Nations to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Africa. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770331_reps_30_hor104/#debate-35)

* Indeed it appears in retrospect that the attitude was taken that it was the responsibility of individuals to escape as best they could, and only when they were out of Vietnam would the Australian Government consider assisting <span class="highlight">refugees</span> . [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770331_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-39-0)

* In view of the Committee's belief that the Australian Government had been informed of the gravity and magnitude of the situation in South Vietnam some 3 weeks before the evacuation of the Australian Embassy, we are unable to come to any conclusion other than one of deliberate delay in order to minimise the number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> with which Australia would have to concern itself. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770331_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-39-0)

* He has been sympathetic to the problem of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and he has set the stage for this country to consider this vital topic, for persons to write to him, for submissions to be made and for community attitudes to be developed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770331_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-39-0)

* It is non-committal on the admittance of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* However, this is another matter and must be taken in context with our moral obligation to accept <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* There is a move to increase the number of  <span class="highlight">refugees</span> entering Australia and details of this are due to be announced shortly in Canberra by the Minister for Immigration and Ethnic Affairs. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* It is interesting to note that in nearly 2 years 2477 war <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Saigon have been admitted to this country, and 4000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> have been admitted from Lebanon since the conflict in that country began. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* Most would agree that <span class="highlight">refugees</span> should be accepted. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* They forget the rising and quite proper expectations and demands of the Third World and our obligations to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from this region, particularly our obligation to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Indo China. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* Political <span class="highlight">refugees</span> also should be given special consideration. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* We should reduce all the difficulties and start to apply a more humane view to the question of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-35-0)

* In December 1974, the previous Government contributed $ I 50,000 to UNICEF to assist in a UNICEF project in Zambia directed at providing humanitarian and educational aid to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> there connected with a number of liberation movements, one of which was SWAPO. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-39-32)

* Did he state on 9 December 1976 (Senate  Hansard  page 2994) that applications for visas to Australia had been received to 25 November 1976 from 1,511 East Timor <span class="highlight">refugees</span> now in Portugal [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-39-58)

* This is evident from official documents on Timorese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Portugal compiled by the Commissariat for Evacuees of the Office of the United Nations High Commissioner for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span> which state that the number of Timorese who arrived in Portugal on evacuation flights totalled 1,392 persons. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770419_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-39-58)

* Every time the question of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> arises we hide behind the United Nations definition, which can be interpreted in whatever way one wishes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770421_reps_30_hor104/#debate-47)

* By hiding behind that definition we can evade our responsibilities, and apply our policy in respect of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in a discriminatory way. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770421_reps_30_hor104/#debate-47)

* Many of our citizens were once <span class="highlight">refugees</span> or displaced persons. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* When we welcomed them, it was hoped that <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and disabled persons were a temporary post-war phenomenon. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* There still are many people in many parts of the world who can be called <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Despite the best efforts of people of good will and of the international community, we must expect that there will continue to be <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* To this end: It has ratified the Convention on the Status of <span class="highlight">Refugees</span>; it is a member of the Executive Committee of the United Nations High Commission for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span> and contributes to the resettlement funds of the UNHCR; it recognises the need through its immigration policy to fulfil the legal obligations required by the Convention and to develop special humanitarian programs for the resettlement of the displaced and/or the persecuted. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* We do injustice to previous governments if we do not give tribute to Australia's contribution in resettlement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in the past. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* If we are to seek to act in the interests of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> themselves and the Australian community, it is necessary to face up to many practical difficulties. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Many <span class="highlight">refugees</span> are not simply migrants beset by a few additional problems. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Those who have in the recent past exhorted the Government to accept greater numbers of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> must take into account the need to coordinate and develop such Government and community resources as will assist not only in the acceptance, but also in the responsible settlement, of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* A fact often forgotten  is  that many <span class="highlight">refugees</span> do not want to come to Australia or, at least, they prefer to go to another country where, for instance, they have close relatives or their language is spoken. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Moreover, our own capacity to accept <span class="highlight">refugees</span> is not unlimited. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Australia's present and future capacity to resettle <span class="highlight">refugees</span> successfully depends on many factors including: The prevailing economic situation; the level of unemployment; the locations within [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Australia to which <span class="highlight">refugees</span> wish to go; the background of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> to be accepted- their capacity for early integration or otherwise; the availability of special post arrival services- language instruction, education, training, accommodation, health and welfare; and the numbers of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> for which voluntary agencies can care. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* The Government's approach to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> is based on the following four principles: [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Australia fully recognises its humanitarian commitment and responsibility to admit <span class="highlight">refugees</span> for resettlement. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* The decision to accept <span class="highlight">refugees</span>- must always remain with the Government of Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Special assistance will often need to be provided for the movement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in designated situations or for their resettlement in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* It may not be in the interest of some <span class="highlight">refugees</span> to settle in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* It is the Government's view that the acceptance and settlement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> should be a continuum beginning with a quick and decisive response to international crises and concluding, after what may be a long and difficult path for the refugee, with successful integration into the Australian community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* We have to recognise, however, that there can be <span class="highlight">refugees</span> with the sort of background, education and skills enabling them to fit readily into the Australian scene. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* It may be a disservice to them to continue to single them out for special treatment as <span class="highlight">refugees</span> after they have arrived in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* There are others who may not wish to be labelled as '<span class="highlight">refugees</span>' over a period. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* In situations where <span class="highlight">refugees</span> are under immediate and dire personal threat, acceptance of people who will face settlement difficulties in Australia is justified. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* More generally, we have to keep in mind that it may not be in the interests of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> not under immediate personal threat to accept them for entry to Australia if they will face major long term settlement problems here. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Within the range of people who are forced by events to become <span class="highlight">refugees</span> there will be many variations of circumstances and conditions. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Some <span class="highlight">refugees</span> will be capable of meeting normal migrant criteria concerning family reunion or occupational skills. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Where appropriate, such <span class="highlight">refugees</span> should be selected and resettled in the normal manner under current migrant policies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Other <span class="highlight">refugees</span> will not fall within the normally acceptable degrees of family relationship or have skills within currently acceptable criteria. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* The interests of those <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who, it is assessed, would have extreme difficulty in adjusting to the Australian environment may not be best served by migration to Australia but be better served by action by the UNHCR or other agencies to resettle them in a more compatible environment. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* There will also be <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, some of working age, who will be unable to qualify for selection under these refugee guidelines because of physical, mental or social handicaps. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Provided that appropriate institutional care is available, Australia will be prepared in principle to accept <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in this category. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Through its ratification of the Convention on the Status of <span class="highlight">Refugees</span>, Australia has accepted certain obligations in relation to people covered by the Convention. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Situations arise from time to time in which people such as those who enter Australia illegally - for example, deserting seamen- or who become prohibited immigrants- for example, by the expiry of temporary permits- claim to be <span class="highlight">refugees</span> entitled to the protection of the Convention and in consequence request permission to remain permanently in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Where it is decided that the Australian response to a refugee situation should be in the form of contributions to the UNHCR or other agencies to resettle or temporarily maintain <span class="highlight">refugees</span> outside Australia, the Minister for Foreign Affairs will continue to determine the modalities and amount of assistance. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* A standing inter-departmental committee on <span class="highlight">refugees</span> comprising a senior officer of the Department of Immigration and Ethnic Affairs as chairman, and senior officers of the Departments of Foreign Affairs, Prime Minister and Cabinet, Employment and Industrial Relations, Social Security, Finance, Health and Education with other departments and the Public Service Board to be co-opted as necessary, will be established. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* This Committee will advise the Minister for Immigration and Ethnic Affairs on the capacity for accepting <span class="highlight">refugees</span>; consult annually, and otherwise as necessary, with voluntary agencies regarding the numbers they would accept for resettlement; recommend co-ordination for arrival and immediate resettlement; and regularly review the intake of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> against the capacity of resources in this country to ensure successful resettlement. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Early consideration will be given to those <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who are the subject of adequate sponsorship by appropriate voluntary bodies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* In this respect there is a continuing flow of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in small groups or as individuals brought to attention by the UNHCR and /or by voluntary agencies in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Provided satisfactory sponsorship is available, a small number of such <span class="highlight">refugees</span> could be accepted on a case by case basis by the Minister for Immigration and Ethnic Affairs. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Some agencies expect they may be able to maintain <span class="highlight">refugees</span> approved for entry to Australia for 12 months after arrival here. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* There will be a regular intake of Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Thailand and nearby areas at a level consistent with our capacity as a community to resettle them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Australia has played, and is continuing to play, a responsible part in the resettlement of distressed persons and <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from the Lebanon and Indo-China. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* -The Opposition welcomes the statement on the Government's policy on <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, belated though it is and with all the shortcomings it contains. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* At least it outlines some machinery for finding some of the facts for investigation in relation to the problems faced by <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and displaced persons throughout the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* For the most part, this long statement is padded with a deal of rhetoric to embellish it as a dramatic and forward move in dealing with the very serious problems of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, quasi-<span class="highlight">refugees</span> and displaced people. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* However, all the purple prose and sophisticated machinery in the world will not go one iota towards resolving the plight of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and other similarly affected people throughout the world unless the Government applies the spirit of the United Nations convention and the spirit of the report which was presented by the Senate Standing Committee on Foreign Affairs and Defence instead of, as it has done up till now, paying lip service to the principles of the convention and hiding behind the legalisms and the literal interpretation of the United Nations definition of 'refugee '. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* The Government is to establish a standing interdepartmental committee on <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, as recommended by the Senate Committee; but it totally ignores the proposal to set up an Australian refugee policy council. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* Membership of this body should be drawn from both government and nongovernment sources- On the non-government side, membership should comprise representatives from the major Australian refugee-receiving and overseas-aid agencies, the Australian representative of the UNHCR (in an observer capacity), Red Cross, other organisations having practical experience in settlement work and post-hostel community support for <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, and representatives from the academic community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* The Government also has ignored its obligations under the convention relating to the status of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* As a means of providing <span class="highlight">refugees</span> (and migrants) with realistic opportunities for obtaining apprenticeships, appropriate employment, admission to tertiary and other educational institutions and opportunities for re-training, the Committee recommends that, irrespective of the current levels of proficiency, financial support be provided to all males and females of working age whilst they attend English language classes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770524_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-29-0)

* What financial help has the Government given or offered to other countries accepting <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and evacuees from Indo-China and East Timor? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780523_reps_31_hor109/#subdebate-3-18)

* Most countries accepting <span class="highlight">refugees</span> for permanent settlement from Indo-China and East Timor are developed countries and therefore would not require financial help from Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780523_reps_31_hor109/#subdebate-3-18)

* Australian bilateral assistance to developing countries who may have accepted <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Indo-China and East Timor is not specifically aimed at helping those countries resettle <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, but is intended to promote their economic and social development. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780523_reps_31_hor109/#subdebate-3-18)

[[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780523_reps_31_hor109/#subdebate-3-18)

* Funds are allocated from this source for assisting <span class="highlight">refugees</span> including those from Indo-China and East Timor. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780523_reps_31_hor109/#subdebate-3-18)

* More recently, Australia has made substantial contributions to UNCHR's Special Program for Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Thailand and other countries in Asia, including the boat people. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780523_reps_31_hor109/#subdebate-3-18)

* Australia also gave $250,000 to the International Committee of the Red Cross in 1975, and $250,000 to the Indonesian Red Cross in 1 976 for the relief of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in East Timor and Indonesian Timor. * It has been said that up to 50,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> have drowned, starved or died of thirst at sea. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790404_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* People seem to forget that <span class="highlight">refugees</span> are people. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790404_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* When I ask these people whether they would prefer <span class="highlight">refugees</span> to be drowned, shot or starved, they have no answer. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790404_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* I bet that the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> wish they did not have this problem. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790404_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* In a number of South East Asian countries, <span class="highlight">refugees</span> are being resettled faster than new arrivals are replacing them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790404_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* What is so different about the present <span class="highlight">refugees</span> that allows them to be treated differently. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790404_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* Noting, in particular, the fact that a great number of them have become <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in their own country or are missing; [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790405_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-26-4)

* Demands the immediate withdrawal of all foreign troops from the Republic of Cyprus and the return of all <span class="highlight">refugees</span> to their homes in freedom and safety; [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790405_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-26-4)

* An additional $3.3m has been included for the Department of Employment and Youth Affairs for the extension of the Community Youth Support Scheme and $3m for the Department of Foreign Affairs for increased contributions under the United Nations High Commission for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> program of assistance for Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790405_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-39-0)

* I refer to reports of a dramatic increase in the number of Kampuchean- formerly Cambodian- <span class="highlight">refugees</span> entering Thailand as a result of fighting between Vietnamese troops and forces loyal to the former Pol Pot regime, and the proposed establishment of a refugee transit centre in Indonesia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* Are <span class="highlight">refugees</span> fleeing the fighting in Kampuchea being denied refuge in Thailand? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* Does the Government support the proposed establishment of an island processing centre for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Indonesia? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* Does the Government support the proposed establishment of a permanent island settlement for <span class="highlight">refugees</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* -There have been a number of recent instances of Kampuchean <span class="highlight">refugees</span> being denied entry into Thailand. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* It is very important, however, to bear in mind that these developments and the other media reports that have referred to this situation should be seen after all against the background of Thailand's long and humanitarian record of granting sanctuary to Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, and its close co-operation with the United [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* Nations High Commission for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span> and other international relief agencies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* The number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in camps supervised by the UNHCR in Thailand alone now exceeds 160,000. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* That takes me to the second part of the honourable member's question, the proposal in January by the Foreign Ministers of the Association of South-East Asian Nations for the establishment of a special island processing centre for Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* Indonesia has offered a site suitable for such a centre with a capacity of 5,000 to 10,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* On the proposition as put forward by the ASEAN Ministers, to which the Government is giving support, we will continue actively to encourage other countries to provide additional resettlement places and financial contributions to the United Nations High Commission for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790502_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-6-0)

* In 1975, his group asked to sponsor 1 1 Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, all Buddhists, at a commune in North Carolina. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790503_reps_31_hor114/#debate-46)

* The <span class="highlight">refugees</span> spent a month with the group, and then left after complaints about their treatment were made to Sen. Jesse Helms, R-N.C. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790503_reps_31_hor114/#debate-46)

* The <span class="highlight">refugees</span> said that they had been worked hard by day, indoctrinated by night in English they did not understand, and prevented from leaving. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790503_reps_31_hor114/#debate-46)

* In addition to the Vietnamese being provided with monetary and technical aid, which enabled them to divert resources to military use, they completely failed to participate in international obligations with regard to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#debate-27)

* They were in fact exporting their problems and exporting <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#debate-27)

* They would not join in the international community activities to stem the flow of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#debate-27)

* There are hundreds of thousands of poor, miserable, wretched <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in camps all round South East Asia because of the direct actions of the Vietnamese Government. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#debate-27)

* I shall confine my remarks to the migration of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from IndoChina to Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-27-0)

* Most of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who are coming to Australia want to live a peaceful life; they do not want to get involved in politics. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-27-0)

* However, there are political elements among the Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-27-0)

* Vo Dai Ton, a former colonel and Deputy Minister of Information in the Thieu regime was described in your article as having tears in his eyes and calling for a band of Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> to go back and 'liberate' Vietnam. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-27-0)

* It is difficult to understand a change of attitude on the part of your paper following the events of Friday 20 April 1979 at which extremist Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> used knives and knuckle dusters to create a riot outside a benefit concert for aid to Vietnam at the Sydney Trades Hall. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-27-0)

* I ask rational people to consider whether this group of extremist <span class="highlight">refugees</span> is capable of achieving what the American military failed to achieve with the expenditure of $35 billion a year. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790510_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-27-0)

* That is important when considering the number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> that Australia can take. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790522_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-16-0)

* We both expressed the view that further reunification of Timorese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> should occur. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790522_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-16-0)

* The problem of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Indo-China is a human problem of vast proportions which affects all of us. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790522_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-54-0)

* Indonesia's co-operation in the IndoChina refugee problem is of importance in maintaining an orderly intake of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> into Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790522_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-54-0)

* Indonesia's continuing help in forestalling unheralded arrivals of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> is very much appreciated, for it is much easier for Australia to take in a significant number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, I believe, when this is done in an orderly way and under proper immigration procedures and not arriving unheralded on our coastline. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790522_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-54-0)

* Indonesia's generous and constructive proposal to establish an island processing centre for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> was discussed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790522_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-54-0)

* ) The United Nations Convention Relating to the Status of <span class="highlight">Refugees</span>, as amended by the Protocol, defines a refugee as a person who, 'owing to a well-founded fear of being persecuted for reasons of race, religion, nationality, membership of a particular social group or political opinion, is outside the country of his nationality and is unable, or owing to such fear, is unwilling to avail himself of the protection of that country; or who, not having a nationality and being outside the country of his former habitual residence, is unable or, owing to such fear, is unwilling to return to it. ' [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790522_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-57-22)

* It is estimated that, since the end of the Vietnam war, some 600,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, mainly of Chinese descent, have fled to neighbouring South East Asian countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* It is very difficult to estimate the figure, but somewhere between 100,000 and 250,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> have perished while seeking refuge. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* As at May 1979, Australia had accepted a total of 20,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> out of this 600,000. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Despite the publicity given to the boat people arriving this year, their total number amounts to no more than one week's intake of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> through normal channels as part of the Government's official refugee program. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* I hope that the Government will continue its present policy which is based on the orderly movement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> through established camps under the auspices of the United Nations High Commissioner for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* The policy, and I support it, is to provide for a controlled intake of 10,500 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> per annum up to the end of 1979-80, by which time some 32,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> will have been accepted. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* It is the equivalent of only one month's outflow of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Vietnam, and I think the public of Australia should view the problem in that perspective. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* The Minister has made it quite clear that there should be no suggestion that more <span class="highlight">refugees</span> means fewer official immigrants. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* But at present we have a responsibly managed and balanced intake which admits families for reunion with persons already in Australia, <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, and persons whose skills can make a positive contribution to the economic development of this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Firstly, quite apart from the compelling humanitarian problems, Australia is one of 77 countries which have become parties to an international convention on the status of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and has therefore taken on certain obligations to assist <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* For example, in 1938 Australia agreed to accept <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Europe, and 7,500 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Germany and Austria arrived in Australia in the 12 months to the middle of 1939. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* From 1939 to 1978 Australia accepted 325,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, including substantial numbers of Poles, Yugoslavs, Hungarians, citizens of the Baltic States, and people from many other corners of the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* It is a global problem requiring a global response, and in the last 12 months or so Australia has accepted <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from some 60 countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* There are about 12 million <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in the world today- nearly equal to the Australian population- the great bulk of whom are seeking refuge from totalitarian regimes which ostensibly have sought to liberate their citizens. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* At the end of April 1979 the number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in transit camps was approaching 300,000. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* My third point is that these <span class="highlight">refugees</span> are located in transit camps in countries with a very limited absorptive capacity which can offer them only a precarious existence, and I should like to quote some very recent figures to illustrate that point. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* In Thailand there are 160,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, including some 14,000 Laotians, 15,000 Kampucheans and 5,000 Vietnamese. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* These are all <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who have crossed borders, and so island transit camps are not going to relieve the situation in Thailand, which is the major country of first refuge. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* There are also 65,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Malaysia and 25,000 in Hong Kong. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Indonesia has approximately 15,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, and in recent months the rate of increase there has been quite alarming. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* There are 4,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in the Philippines, and smaller numbers located elsewhere. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Even if the outflow were to cease immediately, and there is no sign that that will be the case, we know that it would still take another two years to resettle the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> already in camps in this area of the world, assuming that existing promises of resettlement were repeated. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Money is still changing hands, with officials encouraging and organising the departure of large numbers of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* I hope that we will not, for the purposes of international diplomacy, seek to understate the conditions in these countries, thereby making it more difficult for the public to accept the bona fides of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Most <span class="highlight">refugees</span> have suffered discrimination or persecution. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* The sixth point I would like to make is that the development of callous public attitudes to the refugee problem may well cause governments to adopt callous official attitudes to the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> which, in the long term, will have a negative influence on efforts to seek an international solution to the problem. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Recent events in Malaysia and Vietnam itself indicate that several boatloads of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> have been allowed to perish as a result of official action or deliberate inaction. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Although no accurate details are available, it is estimated that as many as 50 per cent of those <span class="highlight">refugees</span> seeking to leave Vietnam have perished while escaping. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* We must therefore continue to meet our international obligations and, at the same time, continue to seek solutions at an international level by supporting, for example, the concept of an island processing centre provided by Indonesia and administered by the UNHCR; by placing pressure on the source countries of Indo-China to have a more compassionate and understanding approach to this problem and, hopefully, to remove the causes of this mass exodus; and finally, by persuading other governments to make greater efforts in offering refuge and resettlement to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* The United States, which has already taken 200,000 Indo-Chinese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, will be taking another 7,000 per month at least until the end of 1980. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* New Zealand is taking only 900 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> per annum. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* After all, it was the Labor Government in 1973 which ratified the 1967 protocol relating to the status of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* This gave official status to its humanitarian obligations to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Yet many honourable members opposite are not prepared to stand up and responsibly support the Government's policy on <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* In my view, if old political divisions remain and continue to dominate public attitudes on this question, it will not only cause further hardship and death to thousands of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, but also it will certainly seriously undermine our strategic position in a corner of the world which is of great significance to the future of Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* I think the House ought to understand the tragic situation in Vietnam, the tragic situation with respect to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>- and there is no one on this side of the House who does not see what has happened in relation to the refugee problem as a tragic outcome. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* The tens of billions of dollars that were expended by the United States in the most inhumane war in modern history has resulted in an extremely tragic situation, not simply for <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who are leaving Vietnam but also for that country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* In relation to the Labor Party seeking to achieve a bipartisan position in relation to <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, I think, on the whole, there has been very little difference. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* I think the Minister for Veterans' Affairs  (Mr Adermann)  who is listening to this debate would say that there is, in fact, very little difference in what the shadow Minister for Immigration has been saying about the way the Australian Government ought to respond to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and what the Minister for Immigration and Ethnic Affairs  (Mr MacKellar)  himself has been saying. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* The Labor Party is no less lacking in compassion with respect to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> than is the Government. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Finally,  Mr Deputy Speaker,  and for only a few minutes, may I take your mind back to this afternoon when in the debate on this Bill the honourable member for Perth  (Mr McLean)  made a very significant address on the issue of Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* I merely want to put on record the fact that the Labor Party when in office had the opportunity to face up to the reality of Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* That opportunity arose towards the end of the Vietnam war when the Labor Government was faced with the issue of whether we would allow to come to Australia Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who, until the end of the war, had in fact worked for the Australian Government. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* We must remember that at that time the Labor Party had an opportunity to deal with the vexed problem of Vietnamese <span class="highlight">refugees</span> and that its response to allowing those unfortunate people to seek a new life in Australia was completely hostile. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790524_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-40-0)

* Has Australia assured Papua New Guinea of Australia's firm support in the event of dispute with Indonesia over granting of political asylum to <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from West Irian. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790531_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-59-8)

* -The Minister for Immigration and Ethnic Affairs will be aware of inquiries from individuals and the community anxious to assist in the support, housing, settlement and adoption of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790604_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-15-0)

* This goodwill is directed towards assisting the resettlement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790604_reps_31_hor114/#subdebate-15-0)
