* Australia had taken from that camp either the third or fourth highest number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-17-0)

* Whilst we are not neglecting our responsibility of taking <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who have gone to Thailand, I believe that there is a need to try to help the boat people who, if they do not get some sort of help at an intermediate stage, might try to make the long trip to Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-17-0)

* We will keep a close eye on the refugee situation in Thailand to which the honourable gentleman referred, but I think we can take some comfort from the fact that we have taken a responsible share of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-17-0)

* Some time ago a group of people with many years of experience in the field of emergency aid (Biafra, Sahel, Bangladesh, Indo China <span class="highlight">refugees</span>) were shocked when they were visiting the area. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791113_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-49-0)

* All of this has put special demands on neighbouring states in the region of Indo-China and has at last attracted world-wide attention to the plight of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791120_reps_31_hor116/#debate-46)

* We spoke with many <span class="highlight">refugees</span>; we spoke with people who had experienced enormous hardship, privation and starvation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* These camps had received enormous numbers of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who had fled by land across the borders. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* We were aware at that stage of the immense pressures building up in Kampuchea for the exodus of an enormous number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The thing that impressed the delegation most of all was the privation and the terrible state of the <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who had fled in enormous numbers across the Kampuchean border into Thailand. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* We had information and were aware that enormous numbers of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> would presently be pushed out. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* There is no doubt whatsoever that the Vietnamese Government is trading in <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* It became obvious to the delegation on the whole of the trip that the action taken by the Australian Government in receiving <span class="highlight">refugees</span> into this country on a permanent basis was enthusiastically received and appreciated. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Concern was expressed that not enough <span class="highlight">refugees</span> were being taken into Australia but we were able to point out that on a per capita basis our track record in this area is the best in the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* It became apparent to me- I speak only for myself on this matter- that the real problem of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in South East Asia, particularly Kampuchea and Vietnam, cannot be solved alone by taking <span class="highlight">refugees</span> into Australia or any other country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I am not talking about 50,000 or 100,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* We are looking at a possible total of one million to two million <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* There is no question that the refugee problem is far bigger than the 37,000 <span class="highlight">refugees</span> we are prepared to take into Australia under our present aid program. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* A substantial number of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> who have come into Australia have made it out of those areas by boat. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Friendly nations are willing to concede 50 per cent of deaths if they say that they will continue to accept <span class="highlight">refugees</span> if they can make it by boat. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791121_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The withdrawal of sanctions leads to recognition of the Rhodesian passport and virtually to the recognition of the entitlement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, whatever race, coming from that area. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Australia would be the area to which <span class="highlight">refugees</span> would come if everything were legitimised and sanctions had been withdrawn. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* We do have a responsibility to the rest of the world, a responsibility we can exercise in many ways by providing the world with food and fibre, providing the world with energy and raw materials, and by responding in a humanitarian way to the plight of the world's poor and hungry people, to the world's <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, especially at the moment in places like Indo-China, and to the people of Timor. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-53-0)

* All Social Security programs, including payments under the Immigration (Guardianship of Children) Act and special benefits for people under maintenance guarantees and for <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, cover migrants insofar as migrants are members of the Australian community. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-55-14)

* The United Nations High Commissioner for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span> has continued his consultations with governments on thus matter and in his latest report to the General Assembly has stated that in the light of these consultations it would appear that the convening of a future session of the conference may be premature at the present. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-57-17)

* 1 ) The intake of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> to Australia is a part of the total immigration program and the Government accepts that, where possible, programs for the settlement of <span class="highlight">refugees</span> should be provided within the context of those for migrants generally. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-57-41)

* It should be noted that <span class="highlight">refugees</span> from Laos and Kampuchea are being resettled in Australia under this program as well as Vietnamese. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-57-41)

* There is a scheme whereby the Commonwealth Government reimburses voluntary agencies for providing needed clothing and other personal requisites to newly-arrived <span class="highlight">refugees</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-57-41)

* Representations have been received from the Hmong- Australia Cultural Society regarding the resettlement in Australia of Hmong <span class="highlight">refugees</span> in Thailand. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-57-41)

* How many persons were approved in the categories, (a) immediate family reunion, (b) special family reunion, (c) nances, (d) independent applicants, (e) employment nominees, (f) <span class="highlight">refugees</span>, (g) patrials, (h) entrepreneurs, (i) self-supporting retirees, and (j) others. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791122_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-57-48)

* I regret that the actions of some South Vietnamese soldiers and officials should have compromised the RAAF in its objectives and in the obligations which it is undertaking to international relief organisations such as the United Nations Children's Emergency Fund and the United Nations High Commissioner for <span class="highlight">Refugees</span>, and obligations which it has to the Government of Malaysia whose air base at Butterworth it uses.
